Wetness is a description of our experience of water; what happens to us when we come into contact with water in such a way that it impinges on our state of being. We, or our possessions, 'get wet'. A less impinging sense experience of water is that it is cold or warm, while visual experience tells us that it is green or blue or muddy or fast-flowing. We learn by experience that a sensation of wetness is associated with water: 'there must be a leak/I must have sat in something.'

general 2022-07-15 12:58:04 Different organisms and differences between animal and plant cells

The origin of life
The Earth formed about 4.6 billion years ago, but life forms may not have formed on Earth until about one billion years later. During the first half of the earth, the atmosphere was thin, different molecules (collection of different or equal atoms that are bound through a chemical bond) were formed by different gas mixtures. These were largely exposed to radiation and powerful electrical charges created by the thunderstorm. Proteins were also synthesized (building up from smaller units) during this. After a while, nucleic acids (biochemical compound that controls the build-up of proteins) formed.
("The Origin of Life", 2020 | "Molecule", 2022 | "Synthesis", 2018 | "Nucleic Acids", 2017)

Photosynthesis
It was not until about 2.5 billion years ago that there were any molecules that through several mutations gained the ability to drive photosynthesis. Photosynthesis is a process in which some cells absorb energy from the sun and convert the inorganic substances carbon dioxide and water into oxygen and glucose (a sugar common in the plant kingdom).
("The Origin of Life", 2020 | "Photosynthesis", 2022 | "Glucose", 2022)

Organimse 1
Organism is a common term for all living things, this then includes animals, plants, fungi and microorganisms. About 2 billion years ago, various types of bacteria that carry out photosynthesis and single-celled algae had produced enough oxygen to drive an oxidative phosphorylation (a chemical energy conversion on which animals depend).
(â€œOrganismâ€; 2020 | â€œThe evolution of life on earthâ€, 2022 | â€œOxidative phosphorylationâ€, 2019)
